-- 表的结构 `bc_delivery`

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `bc_delivery`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `bc_delivery` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `SHIPNO` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '货运单编号',
  `ORDER_ID` int(11) default NULL COMMENT '订单编号',
  `ACCOUNT` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '会员账号',
  `ISPROTECT` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '是否保价',
  `PROTECTPRICE` decimal(20,3) default NULL COMMENT '保价费用',
  `LOGI_ID` int(11) default NULL COMMENT '物流公司Id',
  `MONEY` decimal(20,3) default NULL COMMENT '物流费用',
  `LOGI_NAME` varchar(255) default NULL COMMENT '物流公司名称',
  `LOGI_NO` varchar(255) default NULL COMMENT '配送公司运单号',
  `RECIVER` varchar(255) default NULL COMMENT '收货人',
  `RECIVER_ADDR` varchar(255) default NULL COMMENT '收货地址',
  `RECIVER_ZIP` varchar(50) default NULL COMMENT '邮编',
  `RECIVER_TEL` varchar(50) default NULL COMMENT '收货人电话',
  `RECIVER_MOBILE` varchar(50) default NULL COMMENT '收货人手机',
  `RECIVER_EMAIL` varchar(50) default NULL COMMENT '收货人邮箱',
  `USERID` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '操作员',
  `REMARK` varchar(200) default NULL COMMENT '备注',
  `SENDER` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '送货人',
  `SEND_MOBILE` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '送货人手机',
  `SEND_EMAIL` varchar(50) default NULL COMMENT '送货人邮箱',
  `CREATE_TIME` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '创建时间',
  `REASON` varchar(200) default NULL COMMENT '签收原因',
  `STATUS` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '1发货中，2待签收，3已签收',
  `DISENABLE` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '0 删除  1 正常',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`ID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `bc_fitting`;

  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `GOODSID` int(11) default NULL COMMENT '商品id',
  `CHILDID` int(11) default NULL COMMENT '配件id',
  `NUM` int(11) default NULL COMMENT '数量',

  `CREATER` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '创建者',
  `CREATETIME` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '创建时间',
  `MODIFYDATE` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '最后更新时间',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`ID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- 表的结构 `bc_goods`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `bc_goods`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `bc_goods` (
  `GOODS_ID` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `CODE` varchar(50) default NULL COMMENT '商品编码',
  `NAME` varchar(100) default NULL,
  `SEQCODE` varchar(50) default NULL COMMENT '条形码',
  `SKU` varchar(200) default NULL COMMENT '规格型号',
  `BRAND_ID` int(11) default NULL COMMENT '品牌id',
  `TYPE_ID` int(11) default NULL COMMENT '商品分类id',
  `UNIT` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '计量单位',
  `WEIGHT` decimal(20,3) default NULL COMMENT '重量',
  `MARKET_ENABLE` smallint(1) default NULL COMMENT '0为未上架,1为上架了',
  `MKTPRICE` decimal(20,3) default NULL COMMENT '市场价',
  `PRICE` decimal(20,3) default NULL COMMENT '销售价格',
  `STORE` int(11) default NULL COMMENT '库存',
  `SPECS` varchar(500) default NULL COMMENT '商品规格库存(json格式)',
  `PARAMS` varchar(800) default NULL COMMENT 'json字符串格式',
  `BRIEF` varchar(1000) default NULL COMMENT '简介',
  `NKIND` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '1商品，2既是商品又是配件',
  `ISSALE` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '0不可销售，1可销售',
  `CREATE_TIME` varchar(20) default NULL,
  `LAST_MODIFY` varchar(20) default NULL,
  `VIEW_COUNT` int(10) default NULL,
  `BUY_COUNT` int(10) default NULL,
  `PAGE_TITLE` varchar(255) default NULL,
  `META_KEYWORDS` varchar(200) default NULL,
  `META_DESCRIPTION` varchar(200) default NULL,
  `GYSID` int(11) default NULL COMMENT '供应商id(关联基础信息中供应商表)',
  `PUBLISHER` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '发布人',
  `APPROVER` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '审核人',
  `ATIME` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '审核时间',
  `AREASON` varchar(200) default NULL COMMENT '审核原因',
  `STATUS` smallint(1) default NULL COMMENT '发布状态(1保存，2待发布，3已发布，4取消发布，5拒绝)',
  `PENABLETIME` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '发布生效时间',
  `CANCELPTIME` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '取消发布时间',
  `DISABLED` smallint(1) default NULL COMMENT '0无效，1有效',
  `GOODSURL` varchar(300) default NULL COMMENT '商品信息地址',
  `IMGURL` varchar(100) default NULL COMMENT '图片URL',
  `LISTIMGURL` varchar(500) default NULL COMMENT '缩略图URL',
  `FIRSTPRICE` decimal(20,2) default NULL COMMENT '出厂价',
  `TYPECODE` varchar(50) default NULL COMMENT '分类编码',
  `LOCKSTATUS` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '0未锁定，1锁定',
  `LOCKUSER` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '锁定人',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`GOODS_ID`),
  KEY `GPPDS_BRAND_ID` (`BRAND_ID`),
  KEY `GOODS_NAME` (`NAME`),
  KEY `GOODS_SN` (`CODE`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=364 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- 表的结构 `bc_goods_info`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `bc_goods_info`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `bc_goods_info` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `GOODS_ID` int(11) default NULL,
  `SDESC` text COMMENT '商品介绍',
  `SSPECS` text COMMENT '规格参数',
  `SMETAS` text COMMENT '包装清单',
  `SSEVICE` text COMMENT '售后服务',
  `CREATER` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '创建者',
  `CREATETIME` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '创建时间',
  `MODIFYDATE` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '最后更新时间',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`ID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

--
-- 导出表中的数据 `bc_goods_info`
--


-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- 表的结构 `bc_goods_reviews`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `bc_goods_reviews`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `bc_goods_reviews` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `GOODS_ID` int(11) default NULL,
  `GOODSNAME` varchar(100) default NULL COMMENT '商品名称',
  `ACCOUNT` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '会员帐号',
  `SCONTENT` varchar(400) default NULL COMMENT '评论内容',
  `SIP` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '评论ip',
  `CREATETIME` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '创建时间',
  `NTYPE` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '评论类型(1好评，2中评，3差评)',
  `STATUS` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '0无效，1有效',
  `SCORE` int(11) default NULL COMMENT '评论总分',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`ID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

--
-- 导出表中的数据 `bc_goods_reviews`
--


-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- 表的结构 `bc_goods_specs`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `bc_goods_specs`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `bc_goods_specs` (
  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `GOODSID` int(11) default NULL COMMENT '商品id',
  `CODE` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '货号',
  `PROPS` varchar(1000) default NULL COMMENT '规格（以逗号分隔）',
  `PRICE` decimal(8,3) default NULL COMMENT '单价',
  `STORE` int(11) default NULL COMMENT '库存',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`ID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

--
-- 导出表中的数据 `bc_goods_specs`
--


-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- 表的结构 `bc_goods_type`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `bc_goods_type`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `bc_goods_type` (
  `TYPE_ID` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `SCODE` varchar(60) default NULL COMMENT '编码(每三位代表1级)',
  `NAME` varchar(100) default NULL,
  `KEYWORDS` varchar(200) default NULL,
  `PROPS` varchar(1000) default NULL COMMENT '属性',
  `PARAMS` text COMMENT '参数',
  `DISABLED` smallint(1) default NULL COMMENT '是否可用',
  `HAVE_PROP` smallint(1) default NULL COMMENT '是否有属性',
  `HAVE_PARM` smallint(1) default NULL COMMENT '是否有参数',
  `JOIN_BRAND` smallint(1) default NULL COMMENT '是否关联品牌',
  `NLEVEL` int(3) default NULL COMMENT '第几级分类',
  `CREATER` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '创建者',
  `CREATEDATE` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '创建时间',
  `EDITER` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '最后修改者',
  `EDITDATE` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '最后修改时间',
  `PARENTNO` varchar(100) default NULL COMMENT '上级编码',
  `STATUS` smallint(1) default NULL COMMENT '状态',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`TYPE_ID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=96 ;

-- 表的结构 `bc_integral_rule`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `bc_integral_rule`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `bc_integral_rule` (
  `RULE_ID` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment COMMENT '主键id',
  `RULE_NAME` varchar(200) default NULL COMMENT '积分规则名称',
  `BEGIN_TIME` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '开始时间',
  `END_TIME` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '积分下限',
  `EXPEND_ITURE` decimal(10,2) default NULL COMMENT '积分上限',
  `DISCOUNT` decimal(10,2) default NULL COMMENT '积分系数',
  `INTEGRAL` int(11) default NULL COMMENT '奖励积分',
  `INTEGRAL_TYPE` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '积分类型',
  `STATUS` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '状态',
  `UPDATE_TIME` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '最后更新时间',
  `SDESC` varchar(1000) default NULL COMMENT '描述',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`RULE_ID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=2 ;

--

  `FAX` varchar(30) default NULL,
  `LOGIADDR` varchar(30) default NULL,
  `SHIPFEE` float(10,2) default NULL COMMENT '基本运费',
  `PROTECT` int(1) default NULL,
  `MIN_PRICE` float(10,2) default NULL,
  `PROTECT_RATE` float(6,2) default NULL,
  `HAS_COD` int(1) default NULL,
  `SDESC` varchar(200) default NULL COMMENT '描述',
  `LOCKSTATUS` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '锁定状态: 0 未锁;1 已经锁定',
  `LOCKER` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '锁定人',
  `LOCKTIME` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '锁定时间',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`ID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- 表的结构 `bc_order`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `bc_order`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `bc_order` (
  `ORDER_ID` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `SN` varchar(50) default NULL,
  `ACCOUNT` varchar(30) NOT NULL COMMENT '会员账号',
  `STATUS` smallint(1) NOT NULL COMMENT '1待发货，2发货中，3已发货，4订单完成，7订单取消',
  `PAYSTATUS` smallint(1) default NULL COMMENT '0未付款，1已付款，2已经退款',
  `DELIVERYTYPE` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '配送方式',
  `PAYMENTID` int(11) default NULL COMMENT '支付方式id',
  `PAYMENT_NAME` varchar(50) default NULL COMMENT '支付方式名',
  `RECIVER` varchar(255) default NULL COMMENT '收货人姓名',
  `RECIVERTEL` varchar(50) default NULL COMMENT '收货人电话',
  `RECIVERMOBILE` varchar(50) default NULL COMMENT '收货人手机',
  `RECIVEREMAIL` varchar(50) default NULL COMMENT '收货人邮箱',
  `RECIVERADDR` varchar(255) default NULL COMMENT '收货地址',
  `RECIVERZIP` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '收货人邮编',
  `ISPROTECT` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '是否保价',
  `PROTECTPRICE` decimal(20,3) default NULL COMMENT '保价费用',
  `GOODSAMOUNT` decimal(20,2) default NULL COMMENT '商品总额',
  `SHIPPINGAMOUNT` decimal(20,3) default NULL COMMENT '配送费用',
  `ORDERAMOUNT` decimal(20,3) default NULL COMMENT '订单总额',
  `WEIGHT` decimal(20,3) default NULL COMMENT '商品重量',
  `REMARK` varchar(200) default NULL,
  `PAYMONEY` decimal(20,2) default NULL COMMENT '付款金额',
  `CREATE_TIME` varchar(20) default NULL,
  `ISBILL` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '是否开据发票(0:开据1:不开据)',
  `ORDERTYPE` int(1) NOT NULL COMMENT '订单类型:1.正常订单;2.积分兑换单;3手工订单',
  `PAYSORT` int(2) NOT NULL default '1' COMMENT '付款类型，1 在线支付，0 货到付款 20 积分兑换',
  `USERID` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '用于记录当前锁定订单的业务人员，登录的用户名',
  `OLOCK` int(1) default '0' COMMENT '1 已经锁定， 0 未锁',
  `LOCKTIME` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '锁定与解锁时间',
  `CANCELTIME` varchar(20) default NULL,
  `DISABLED` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '删除标志:0已删除1未删除',
  `FINISHEDTIME` varchar(20) default NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`ORDER_ID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COMMENT='订单' AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

--
-- 导出表中的数据 `bc_order`
--

  `LOGTYPE` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '1 流程日志，0 锁定与解锁日志',
  `ORDER_TYPE` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '订单类型',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`LOG_ID`)

  `ID` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `NAME` varchar(50) default NULL,
  `CONFIG` varchar(1000) default NULL,
  `BIREF` varchar(200) default NULL COMMENT '描述',
  `PAY_FEE` decimal(20,2) default NULL COMMENT '费率',
  `TYPE` varchar(255) default NULL COMMENT 'alipay,tenpay,offline,deposit',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`ID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- 表的结构 `group_purchase`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `group_purchase`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `group_purchase` (
  `GPID` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment COMMENT '主键',
  `GPTITLE` varchar(128) default NULL COMMENT '团购标题',
  `GOODSCODE` varchar(50) default NULL COMMENT '商品编码，选择自商品信息表或组合商品信息表，也可自动生成，自动生成时相当于商品来至供货商，自动生成商品编码T开头；例如：T000000001。',
  `SPID` int(11) default NULL COMMENT '供应商，来至供应商表',
  `PTID` int(11) default NULL COMMENT '团购商品类型',
  `CTIME` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '维护时间',
  `FREIGHT` smallint(1) default '0' COMMENT '是否需要运费，1 需要运费，0免运费',
  `SEQ` int(10) default NULL COMMENT '排序，同一天团购排序，1最前。',
  `WEIGHT` decimal(20,3) default NULL COMMENT '重量，选择已存在的商品可将重量带过来',
  `INTEGRAL` int(10) default NULL COMMENT '积分数量，团购积分值。',
  `PRICE` decimal(20,3) default NULL COMMENT '市场价格',
  `GPRICE` decimal(20,3) default NULL COMMENT '团购价格',
  `IMAGE` varchar(300) default NULL COMMENT '图片',
  `STORENUMBER` int(10) default NULL COMMENT '库存数量，团购对客户显示的可购买数量',
  `MAXNUMBER` int(10) default NULL COMMENT '最大购买数量',
  `MINPEOPLE` int(10) default NULL COMMENT '团购起始人数',
  `BEGINTIME` datetime default NULL COMMENT '起始时间',
  `ENDTIME` datetime default NULL COMMENT '团购过期时间，指非直销团购，例如团购卷等。团购过期时间',
  `CLOSETIME` datetime default NULL COMMENT '团购过期时间， 非直销商品例如：券有效期',
  `BUYONCE` smallint(1) default '0' COMMENT '1 只能购买一次，0 可多次购买 BUYONCE，默认0可多次购买',
  `CARD` decimal(20,3) default NULL COMMENT '代金卷可使用额度，0 不可使用代金卷。字段预留',
  `SUMMARY` text COMMENT '站内对商品的简要描述',
  `DETAIL` text COMMENT '商品详细描述',
  `STATE` varchar(20) default 'normal' COMMENT 'normal 正常，success 团购成功，failure 失败，refund 退货；例如：未达到团购人数',
  `BOUGHTNUM` int(8) default NULL COMMENT '购买人数',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`GPID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COMMENT='团购信息维护' AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

--
-- 导出表中的数据 `group_purchase`

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `pmt_groupgoods`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `pmt_groupgoods` (
  `GGID` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment COMMENT '系统编码，系统生成',
  `GGCODE` varchar(50) NOT NULL COMMENT '组合商品编码，以固定数字开头，暂定 数字9开头；可自动生成，例如9000000001',
  `GGNAME` varchar(100) NOT NULL COMMENT '组合商品名称',
  `GGBARCODE` varchar(50) default NULL COMMENT '条码，如果物品编码GGCODE相同，条码一定相同的，并且不可修改；预留',
  `GGPRICE` decimal(20,3) NOT NULL COMMENT '组合商品价格',
  `IMGURL` varchar(200) default NULL COMMENT '组合商品url',
  `GGSTARTTIME` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '起始时间',
  `GGENDTIME` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '截止时间，',
  `GGVALID` smallint(1) NOT NULL default '1' COMMENT '有效标识，1有效，0无效，默认1',
  `USERID` int(11) default NULL COMMENT '创建人',
  `GGCTIME` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '创建时间',
  `GGEUSER` int(11) default NULL COMMENT '修改人',
  `GGETIME` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '修改时间',
  `GGAUDITOR` int(11) default NULL COMMENT '审核人',
  `GGAUDITTIME` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '审核时间',
  `GGAUDITSTATUS` smallint(1) default '3' COMMENT '审核状态，3 待审核，1 通过, 0 拒绝。默认为3',
  `GGCHANGEDRECORD` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '组合商品变更记录 ，对审核状态为 1的（审核通过的组合商品），进行修改时记录原来组合上边的编码。；新增时为空',
  `GGMEMO` varchar(500) default NULL COMMENT '备注',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`GGID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COMMENT='组合物品主表' AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

  `SDESC` varchar(500) default NULL,

) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

--
-- 表的结构 `sys_role`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `sys_role`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `sys_role` (
  `ROLEID` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment COMMENT '角色编号',
  `ROLENAME` varchar(100) default NULL COMMENT '角色名称',
  `ROLEDESC` varchar(200) default NULL COMMENT '描述',
  `ROLETYPE` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '角色类型(0超级管理员，1用户)',
  `ROLEORGCODE` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '角色所属区域编码',
  `ROLEENABLE` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '角色有效性(1有效，0无效)',
  `CREATER` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '创建人',
  `CREATETIME` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '创建时间',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`ROLEID`),
  KEY `INDEX_ROLE_ROLENAME` (`ROLENAME`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=3 ;

--
-- 导出表中的数据 `sys_role`
--

INSERT INTO `sys_role` (`ROLEID`, `ROLENAME`, `ROLEDESC`, `ROLETYPE`, `ROLEORGCODE`, `ROLEENABLE`, `CREATER`, `CREATETIME`) VALUES
(1, '管理员', '管理员', 0, NULL, 1, 'admin', '2011-05-04 20:11:33'),
(2, '一般人员', '一般角色', 1, NULL, 1, 'admin', '2012-01-12 15:56:55');

--
-- 表的结构 `sys_user`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `sys_user`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `sys_user` (
  `USERID` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment COMMENT '用户编号',
  `USERACCOUNT` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '登陆名',
  `USERNAME` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '真实姓名',
  `USERPWD` varchar(32) default NULL COMMENT '密码',
  `USERSEX` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '性别 0男1女',
  `USERIMG` varchar(100) default NULL COMMENT '用户电子照片地址',
  `USERBOTH` varchar(18) default NULL COMMENT '出生年月日',
  `USERJOB` varchar(40) default NULL COMMENT '职位',
  `USERTEL` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '电话',
  `USERFAX` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT '传真',
  `USERMP` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '手机',
  `USEREMAIL` varchar(50) default NULL COMMENT '邮箱',
  `USERQQ` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT 'QQ',
  `USERMSN` varchar(30) default NULL COMMENT 'msn',
  `USERCITY` varchar(20) default NULL COMMENT '用户所在城市',
  `USERTYPE` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '用户类型(0普能，1会员)',
  `USERLEVEL` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '用户级别',
  `USERCREATEDATE` varchar(18) default NULL COMMENT '创建日期',
  `USERDESC` varchar(200) default NULL COMMENT '用户描述',
  `ISENABLE` int(1) default NULL COMMENT '用户有效性（1有效，0无效）',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`USERID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=4 ;

-- 导出表中的数据 `sys_user`
--

--
-- Stand-in structure for view `v_goods`
--
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `v_goods` (
`goods_id` int(11)
,`code` varchar(50)
,`name` varchar(100)
,`seqcode` varchar(50)
,`sku` varchar(200)
,`brand_id` int(11)
,`type_id` int(11)
,`unit` varchar(20)
,`weight` decimal(20,3)
,`market_enable` smallint(1)
,`mktprice` decimal(20,3)
,`price` decimal(20,3)
,`store` int(11)
,`specs` varchar(500)
,`params` varchar(800)
,`brief` varchar(1000)
,`nkind` int(1)
,`issale` int(1)
,`create_time` varchar(20)
,`last_modify` varchar(20)
,`view_count` int(10)
,`buy_count` int(10)
,`page_title` varchar(255)
,`meta_keywords` varchar(200)
,`meta_description` varchar(200)
,`gysid` int(11)
,`publisher` varchar(30)
,`approver` varchar(30)
,`atime` varchar(30)
,`areason` varchar(200)
,`status` smallint(1)
,`penabletime` varchar(30)
,`cancelptime` varchar(30)
,`disabled` smallint(1)
,`goodsurl` varchar(300)
,`imgurl` varchar(100)
,`listimgurl` varchar(500)
,`firstprice` decimal(20,2)
,`typecode` varchar(50)
,`typename` varchar(100)
,`brandname` varchar(50)
,`typestatus` smallint(1)
,`brandstatus` smallint(1)
,`tagid` int(11)
,`tag_name` varchar(255)
,`tag_type` varchar(255)
,`rel_count` int(11)
);

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure for view `v_goods`
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `v_goods`;

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS `v_goods`;
CREATE ALGORITHM=UNDEFINED DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` SQL SECURITY DEFINER VIEW `gxadmin`.`v_goods` AS select `bg`.`GOODS_ID` AS `goods_id`,`bg`.`CODE` AS `code`,`bg`.`NAME` AS `name`,`bg`.`SEQCODE` AS `seqcode`,`bg`.`SKU` AS `sku`,`bg`.`BRAND_ID` AS `brand_id`,`bg`.`TYPE_ID` AS `type_id`,`bg`.`UNIT` AS `unit`,`bg`.`WEIGHT` AS `weight`,`bg`.`MARKET_ENABLE` AS `market_enable`,`bg`.`MKTPRICE` AS `mktprice`,`bg`.`PRICE` AS `price`,`bg`.`STORE` AS `store`,`bg`.`SPECS` AS `specs`,`bg`.`PARAMS` AS `params`,`bg`.`BRIEF` AS `brief`,`bg`.`NKIND` AS `nkind`,`bg`.`ISSALE` AS `issale`,`bg`.`CREATE_TIME` AS `create_time`,`bg`.`LAST_MODIFY` AS `last_modify`,`bg`.`VIEW_COUNT` AS `view_count`,`bg`.`BUY_COUNT` AS `buy_count`,`bg`.`PAGE_TITLE` AS `page_title`,`bg`.`META_KEYWORDS` AS `meta_keywords`,`bg`.`META_DESCRIPTION` AS `meta_description`,`bg`.`GYSID` AS `gysid`,`bg`.`PUBLISHER` AS `publisher`,`bg`.`APPROVER` AS `approver`,`bg`.`ATIME` AS `atime`,`bg`.`AREASON` AS `areason`,`bg`.`STATUS` AS `status`,`bg`.`PENABLETIME` AS `penabletime`,`bg`.`CANCELPTIME` AS `cancelptime`,`bg`.`DISABLED` AS `disabled`,`bg`.`GOODSURL` AS `goodsurl`,`bg`.`IMGURL` AS `imgurl`,`bg`.`LISTIMGURL` AS `listimgurl`,`bg`.`FIRSTPRICE` AS `firstprice`,`bg`.`TYPECODE` AS `typecode`,`bgt`.`NAME` AS `typename`,`bb`.`NAME` AS `brandname`,`bgt`.`DISABLED` AS `typestatus`,`bb`.`DISABLED` AS `brandstatus`,`btr`.`TAGID` AS `tagid`,`bt`.`TAG_NAME` AS `tag_name`,`bt`.`TAG_TYPE` AS `tag_type`,`bt`.`REL_COUNT` AS `rel_count` from ((((`gxadmin`.`bc_goods` `bg` left join `gxadmin`.`bc_goods_type` `bgt` on((`bg`.`TYPECODE` = `bgt`.`SCODE`))) left join `gxadmin`.`bc_brand` `bb` on((`bg`.`BRAND_ID` = `bb`.`BRAND_ID`))) left join `gxadmin`.`bc_tag_rel` `btr` on((`bg`.`GOODS_ID` = `btr`.`GOODSID`))) left join `gxadmin`.`bc_tags` `bt` on((`bt`.`TAG_ID` = `btr`.`TAGID`))) where ((`bg`.`DISABLED` = 1) and (`bg`.`ISSALE` = 1));

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure for view `v_goods_tag`
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `v_goods_tag`;

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS `v_goods_tag`;
CREATE ALGORITHM=UNDEFINED DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` SQL SECURITY DEFINER VIEW `gxadmin`.`v_goods_tag` AS select `bg`.`GOODS_ID` AS `goods_id`,`bg`.`CODE` AS `code`,`bg`.`NAME` AS `name`,`bg`.`SEQCODE` AS `seqcode`,`bg`.`SKU` AS `sku`,`bg`.`BRAND_ID` AS `brand_id`,`bg`.`TYPE_ID` AS `type_id`,`bg`.`UNIT` AS `unit`,`bg`.`WEIGHT` AS `weight`,`bg`.`MARKET_ENABLE` AS `market_enable`,`bg`.`MKTPRICE` AS `mktprice`,`bg`.`PRICE` AS `price`,`bg`.`STORE` AS `store`,`bg`.`SPECS` AS `specs`,`bg`.`PARAMS` AS `params`,`bg`.`BRIEF` AS `brief`,`bg`.`NKIND` AS `nkind`,`bg`.`ISSALE` AS `issale`,`bg`.`CREATE_TIME` AS `create_time`,`bg`.`LAST_MODIFY` AS `last_modify`,`bg`.`VIEW_COUNT` AS `view_count`,`bg`.`BUY_COUNT` AS `buy_count`,`bg`.`PAGE_TITLE` AS `page_title`,`bg`.`META_KEYWORDS` AS `meta_keywords`,`bg`.`META_DESCRIPTION` AS `meta_description`,`bg`.`GYSID` AS `gysid`,`bg`.`PUBLISHER` AS `publisher`,`bg`.`APPROVER` AS `approver`,`bg`.`ATIME` AS `atime`,`bg`.`AREASON` AS `areason`,`bg`.`STATUS` AS `status`,`bg`.`PENABLETIME` AS `penabletime`,`bg`.`CANCELPTIME` AS `cancelptime`,`bg`.`DISABLED` AS `disabled`,`btr`.`TAGID` AS `tagid`,`bt`.`TAG_NAME` AS `tag_name`,`bt`.`TAG_TYPE` AS `tag_type`,`bt`.`REL_COUNT` AS `rel_count` from ((`gxadmin`.`bc_goods` `bg` left join `gxadmin`.`bc_tag_rel` `btr` on((`bg`.`GOODS_ID` = `btr`.`GOODSID`))) left join `gxadmin`.`bc_tags` `bt` on((`bt`.`TAG_ID` = `btr`.`TAGID`)));

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure for view `v_goods_type`
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `v_goods_type`;

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS `v_goods_type`;
CREATE ALGORITHM=UNDEFINED DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` SQL SECURITY DEFINER VIEW `gxadmin`.`v_goods_type` AS select `bg`.`GOODS_ID` AS `goods_id`,`bg`.`CODE` AS `code`,`bg`.`NAME` AS `name`,`bg`.`SEQCODE` AS `seqcode`,`bg`.`SKU` AS `sku`,`bg`.`BRAND_ID` AS `brand_id`,`bg`.`TYPE_ID` AS `type_id`,`bg`.`UNIT` AS `unit`,`bg`.`WEIGHT` AS `weight`,`bg`.`MARKET_ENABLE` AS `market_enable`,`bg`.`MKTPRICE` AS `mktprice`,`bg`.`PRICE` AS `price`,`bg`.`STORE` AS `store`,`bg`.`SPECS` AS `specs`,`bg`.`PARAMS` AS `params`,`bg`.`BRIEF` AS `brief`,`bg`.`NKIND` AS `nkind`,`bg`.`ISSALE` AS `issale`,`bg`.`CREATE_TIME` AS `create_time`,`bg`.`LAST_MODIFY` AS `last_modify`,`bg`.`VIEW_COUNT` AS `view_count`,`bg`.`BUY_COUNT` AS `buy_count`,`bg`.`PAGE_TITLE` AS `page_title`,`bg`.`META_KEYWORDS` AS `meta_keywords`,`bg`.`META_DESCRIPTION` AS `meta_description`,`bg`.`GYSID` AS `gysid`,`bg`.`PUBLISHER` AS `publisher`,`bg`.`APPROVER` AS `approver`,`bg`.`ATIME` AS `atime`,`bg`.`AREASON` AS `areason`,`bg`.`STATUS` AS `status`,`bg`.`PENABLETIME` AS `penabletime`,`bg`.`CANCELPTIME` AS `cancelptime`,`bg`.`DISABLED` AS `disabled`,`bg`.`GOODSURL` AS `goodsurl`,`bg`.`IMGURL` AS `imgurl`,`bg`.`LISTIMGURL` AS `listimgurl`,`bg`.`FIRSTPRICE` AS `firstprice`,`bg`.`TYPECODE` AS `typecode`,`bgt`.`NAME` AS `typename`,`bb`.`NAME` AS `brandname`,`bgt`.`DISABLED` AS `typestatus`,`bb`.`DISABLED` AS `brandstatus` from ((`gxadmin`.`bc_goods` `bg` left join `gxadmin`.`bc_goods_type` `bgt` on((`bg`.`TYPECODE` = `bgt`.`SCODE`))) left join `gxadmin`.`bc_brand` `bb` on((`bg`.`BRAND_ID` = `bb`.`BRAND_ID`))) where ((`bg`.`DISABLED` = 1) and (`bg`.`ISSALE` = 1));

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure for view `v_menurights`
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `v_menurights`;

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS `v_menurights`;
CREATE ALGORITHM=UNDEFINED DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` SQL SECURITY DEFINER VIEW `gxadmin`.`v_menurights` AS select `m`.`MENUCODE` AS `MENUCODE`,`m`.`MENUNAME` AS `MENUNAME`,`m`.`MENUENNAME` AS `MENUENNAME`,`m`.`PARENTMENUCODE` AS `PARENTMENUCODE`,`m`.`MENUURL` AS `MENUURL`,`m`.`MENUFLAG` AS `MENUFLAG`,`m`.`SEQU` AS `SEQU`,`m`.`MENUENABLE` AS `MENUENABLE`,`m`.`SYSMARK` AS `SYSMARK`,`r`.`ROLEID` AS `roleid` from ((`gxadmin`.`sys_menu` `m` join `gxadmin`.`sys_role` `r`) join `gxadmin`.`sys_role_menu` `rm`) where ((`m`.`MENUCODE` = `rm`.`MENUCODE`) and (`r`.`ROLEID` = `rm`.`ROLEID`));

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure for view `v_storevo`
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `v_storevo`;

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS `v_storevo`;
CREATE ALGORITHM=UNDEFINED DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` SQL SECURITY DEFINER VIEW `gxadmin`.`v_storevo` AS select `b`.`GOODS_ID` AS `GOODS_ID`,`b`.`CODE` AS `CODE`,`b`.`NAME` AS `NAME`,`b`.`SEQCODE` AS `SEQCODE`,`b`.`SKU` AS `SKU`,`b`.`BRAND_ID` AS `BRAND_ID`,`b`.`TYPE_ID` AS `TYPE_ID`,`b`.`UNIT` AS `UNIT`,`b`.`WEIGHT` AS `WEIGHT`,`b`.`MARKET_ENABLE` AS `MARKET_ENABLE`,`b`.`MKTPRICE` AS `MKTPRICE`,`b`.`PRICE` AS `PRICE`,`b`.`STORE` AS `STORE`,`b`.`SPECS` AS `SPECS`,`b`.`PARAMS` AS `PARAMS`,`b`.`BRIEF` AS `BRIEF`,`b`.`NKIND` AS `NKIND`,`b`.`ISSALE` AS `ISSALE`,`b`.`CREATE_TIME` AS `CREATE_TIME`,`b`.`LAST_MODIFY` AS `LAST_MODIFY`,`b`.`VIEW_COUNT` AS `VIEW_COUNT`,`b`.`BUY_COUNT` AS `BUY_COUNT`,`b`.`PAGE_TITLE` AS `PAGE_TITLE`,`b`.`META_KEYWORDS` AS `META_KEYWORDS`,`b`.`META_DESCRIPTION` AS `META_DESCRIPTION`,`b`.`GYSID` AS `GYSID`,`b`.`PUBLISHER` AS `PUBLISHER`,`b`.`APPROVER` AS `APPROVER`,`b`.`ATIME` AS `ATIME`,`b`.`AREASON` AS `AREASON`,`b`.`STATUS` AS `STATUS`,`b`.`PENABLETIME` AS `PENABLETIME`,`b`.`CANCELPTIME` AS `CANCELPTIME`,`b`.`DISABLED` AS `DISABLED`,`b`.`GOODSURL` AS `GOODSURL`,`b`.`IMGURL` AS `IMGURL`,`b`.`LISTIMGURL` AS `LISTIMGURL`,`s`.`NAME` AS `SUPPLIERNAME`,`s`.`ADDRESS` AS `ADDRESS`,`s`.`LINKMAN` AS `LINKMAN`,`s`.`LINKMOBILE` AS `LINKMOBILE`,`s`.`LINKEMAIL` AS `LINKEMAIL`,`s`.`LINKTEL` AS `LINKTEL`,`s`.`FAX` AS `FAX` from (`gxadmin`.`bc_goods` `b` left join `gxadmin`.`bc_supplier` `s` on((`b`.`GYSID` = `s`.`ID`)));

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure for view `v_userrole`
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `v_userrole`;

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS `v_userrole`;
CREATE ALGORITHM=UNDEFINED DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` SQL SECURITY DEFINER VIEW `gxadmin`.`v_userrole` AS select distinct `u`.`USERID` AS `userid`,`u`.`USERACCOUNT` AS `useraccount`,`r`.`ROLEID` AS `roleid` from ((`gxadmin`.`sys_user` `u` join `gxadmin`.`sys_role` `r`) join `gxadmin`.`sys_user_role` `ur`) where ((`u`.`USERID` = `ur`.`USERID`) and (`r`.`ROLEID` = `ur`.`ROLEID`));
